989 <h2>Learn About Design from Professional Interior Designers</h2>

990 <p>Whats the difference between modern and contemporary? What is transitional design? How do you know which design is right for you? We researched the most popular interior design styles, along with the definition, history, and characteristics of each. We interviewed multiple design and home professionals around the country to bring in multiple perspectives.</p>

991 <p>You can choose one specific design for your entire house or select a unique style for each room. Each product you select contributes to the design of your space, from lighting to flooring and everything in between. Explore our simple guides to see which design fits your vision best or use it for inspiration, then browse our website to find the right products for your design.</p>

992 </div>

1036 <h3>Your Design 101 Questions Answered</h3>

1037 <p>Still deciding on a design style for your remodel? Our easy guides take the guesswork out of selecting a design while our articles demonstrate the unique aspects of each aesthetic. We walk through distinctive elements such as color palettes, shapes, fixture finishes, and more. Discover the latest contemporary design trends, or fall in love with a classic, timeless design.</p>

1038 <p>No matter what style you gravitate towards, our guides translate your design goals into products. Have suggestions for which style we should write about next? We would love to know your thoughts, suggestions, and questions. Send us an email at

1039 <a href="mailto:design@vevano.com">design@vevano.com</a>.
